<script>
    var mybutton = document.getElementById("myBtn");
    window.onscroll = function() {
        scrollFunction()
    };
    function scrollFunction() {
        if (document.body.scrollTop > 20 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 20) {
            mybutton.style.display = "block";
        } else {
            mybutton.style.display = "none";
        }
    }
    function topFunction() {
        document.body.scrollTop = 0;
        document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0;
    }

    $('.toggleButton').click(function() {
        $('.my-sticky-div').toggleClass('bottom');
    });
</script>

<script data-ad-client="ca-pub-6081967606533178" data-src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js" data-type="lazy" src="https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js" data-checked-head="true"></script>
<script id="flying-scripts" type="text/javascript">
    const userInteractionEvents = ["mouseover", "keydown", "touchstart", "touchmove", "wheel"];
    userInteractionEvents.forEach(function(event) {
        window.addEventListener(event, triggerScriptLoader, {
            passive: !0
        })
    });

    function triggerScriptLoader() {
        loadScripts();
        userInteractionEvents.forEach(function(event) {
            window.removeEventListener(event, triggerScriptLoader, {
                passive: !0
            })
        })
    }

    function loadScripts() {
        document.querySelectorAll("script[data-type='lazy']").forEach(function(elem) {
            elem.setAttribute("src", elem.getAttribute("data-src"))
        })
    }
</script>

                event.preventDefault();
            }
        });

        <script>
            initiateCodes();
            appendExtraFiles();
            // append extra JS files
            function appendExtraFiles() {
                var jsFiles = [
                    "https://www.online-notepad.net/assets/js/jquery-ui.min.js",
                    "https://www.online-notepad.net/assets/ck-edit/sample/ckeditor.js?v=1.0.2",
                    "https://www.online-notepad.net/assets/js/notes.js?v=1.0.8"
                ];

                setTimeout(function() {
                    var bodyID = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
                    for (let index = 0; index < jsFiles.length; index++) {
                        var newScript = document.createElement('script');
                        newScript.type = 'text/javascript';
                        newScript.src = jsFiles[index];
                        bodyID.appendChild(newScript);
                    }
                }, 2000);
            }

            function initiateCodes(){

                setTimeout(function(){
                    // initial rich editor
                    DecoupledDocumentEditor
                    .create(document.querySelector('#editor'), {
                        extraPlugins: [SimpleUploadAdapter],
                        removePlugins: ['MediaEmbed']
                    })
                    .then(editor => {
                        const toolbarContainer = document.querySelector('main .toolbar-container');

                        toolbarContainer.prepend(editor.ui.view.toolbar.element);

                        window.editor = editor;
                    })
                    .catch(err => {
                        console.error(err.stack);
                    });

                    // initiate sortable
                    $(function() {
                        $("#sortable").sortable();
                    });
                },2500)
            }
            $(".choosedLang").on('click',function(){
                const selectedURL = $(this).data('href');
            })
        </script>
